# 中国出租车大全｜轻井泽惠

来源：https://www.yuque.com/chaofun/tuxun/cn_taxi_all

## 前言

- 本文档统计了街景车拍摄的有出租车出现的街景（包含百度、腾讯、谷歌街景），部分县、区可能因为无街景车拍摄、无出租车公司、街景中无法找到出租车等原因无出租车图片，如果发现文档有遗漏的出租车图片欢迎在文档下方评论区贴出街景链接，我会尽快添加。

- 由于精力有限，本文档仅对出租车涂装进行统计，如果想学习主要城市出租车涂装与车型可以点击以下文档[全国主要城市出租车｜何以为龢](https://www.yuque.com/chaofun/tuxun/cn_taxi1)。

- 本文档只供玩家学习使用，请不要在申诉时才使用本文档。

- 可以点击以下[题库](https://tuxun.fun/map/29062)进行游玩。

## 北京

### 北京市

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/38582148/1749139287050-510361e5-f248-44b2-8049-a3081d75794f.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_24%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/38582148/1749139331738-aec6a0ec-bbe8-4d19-b0cd-9b51695af082.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_23%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/38582148/1749139358134-1153ea2b-32e3-4ddc-b189-6cc04ca6ba46.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_22%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/38582148/1749139376089-6211895a-66f1-4c6a-9a06-4c9685305205.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_30%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/38582148/1749139404659-1a7590ec-4955-4c55-9b51-26738e27d5b7.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_36%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

中间为橙黄色，上下两边颜色不定，在北京所有区均有覆盖。全国很多地方的出租车采用这类涂装。

## 天津

### 天津市

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/38582148/1749221270085-030a7f48-6f40-4b54-afc6-fec2171044c4.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_25%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

所有天津市辖区均有此款涂装，该涂装在全国范围内十分常见。

## 黑龙江

### 哈尔滨

#### 哈尔滨市

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1732117286387-e3276993-9a47-4ec9-91b7-2a57c01a335b.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_14%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

可通过前车牌上方的白色牌子进行辨认。

#### 宾县

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1732118084330-9f708cbc-7327-4616-9d3a-4fae1f8f583e.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_15%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

上半部为红色，其余与哈尔滨市相同，包括前车牌上端白色牌子。

### 抚顺

#### 抚顺市

### 唐山

#### 唐山市

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1733235092071-f505e25b-4666-4256-88c3-2f84f7c63748.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_15%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1733235279659-e70f9824-9fc0-4afc-aa55-024d6e2468a4.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_10%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

涂装较多，第一种最为常见。

#### 丰润区

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1733235438044-e8574fda-26c8-4bdb-887e-ead7de4f9494.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_12%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

古冶区有相同的涂装。

#### 曹妃甸区

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1733320507305-531ed02a-b0ce-44b4-a7d6-29eaa19f0b13.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_15%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

车门印有”曹妃甸出租“，可以记一下公司标志。

#### 遵化市

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1733321008104-d1824732-217d-487e-91b4-1a4235a205f3.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_13%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

第一种涂装较为常见。

#### 迁安市

#### 滦州市

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1733321446386-1a472d3b-e8af-489d-b0ea-d65ede4a0394.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_17%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

与曹妃甸出租车涂装极为相似，可通过公司标志区分。

#### 滦南县

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1733321656974-6a8a91be-8a19-466a-b213-f09cf32b6a9d.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_11%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1733321679086-943e33d0-4094-4d2f-a93b-2c3bb8b7f7b2.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_11%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

和滦州市出租车涂装有些许的不同。

#### 乐亭县

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1733322034470-cd58804b-9671-463d-86f7-f4c70517670a.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_19%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

除了车顶灯牌不一样，和其它县区的涂装几乎一致。

### 张家口

#### 张家口市

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1733490852321-3d8486e8-e858-4dae-bffa-a0eb21aaabdc.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_11%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

注意车身白色线条。

#### 万全区

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1733491023155-d887d768-350c-4393-b9fe-ea1da2637fa6.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_15%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

注意车门上的黄色标志，主城区出租也相当常见。

钢城区也是同一款涂装。

### 淄博

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1733627188710-7db833a4-136a-45f6-9f8c-5764e3ebc3c7.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_15%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

### 鹤壁

#### 鹤壁市

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1734259642656-21dd7634-5295-4a3c-a196-8df44e5e5ba2.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_21%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 浚县

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1734260514229-f9f630d0-11b7-4280-9128-f964f6af6867.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_14%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 淇县

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1734260678740-f4d8ceb2-1105-42fc-a766-2545f669b3b5.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_16%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

与浚县出租车涂装十分相似，区别在于前车牌无绿色半圆牌子。

### 焦作

#### 焦作市

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1734266674584-ee5337f5-a6a7-4b37-87d2-e70dba70f932.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_20%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 修武县

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2024/png/38582148/1734267399039-1db1869c-a97e-43a2-ad44-b5558a91c80c.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_22%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

和宿迁市区出租车涂装有些许不同。

## 重庆

### 重庆市

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/38582148/1742997286623-130dbd5f-52b9-4dfe-9789-476606c8d1c9.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_17%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

主城区基本都为此款黄色法拉利，车顶灯牌竖向摆放。

### 璧山区

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/38582148/1742305223414-8b4c4618-ecdf-4d37-9867-38f96feaab1e.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_24%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

#### 察哈尔右翼前旗

![image.png](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/38582148/1747745852232-c22dcbf4-2046-4289-ba57-69e2682ebf8c.png?x-oss-process=image%2Fwatermark%2Ctype_d3F5LW1pY3JvaGVp%2Csize_24%2Ctext_VHV4dW5Eb2M%3D%2Ccolor_FFFFFF%2Cshadow_50%2Ct_80%2Cg_se%2Cx_10%2Cy_10)

无固定车型及涂装，车顶有小形出租车灯牌，仍可见大量集宁区出租车。

#### 察哈尔右翼中旗

有着十余种涂装，车尾写有不同的休息日期，可以从多辆出租车中推断街景拍摄于周几。

## 西藏

### 拉萨

前两款最为常见，前车牌顶部有绿色牌子。
